[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m631[0m[39m:                default:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m632[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mreadPrivate[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey, [0m[1;35mreadDictValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m633[0m[39m:                    break;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m634[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m635[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m636[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m637[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m some fonts have [0m[32m"2 index"[0m[39m here, others have [0m[32m"end noaccess put"[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m638[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m sometimes followed by [0m[32m"put"[0m[39m. Either way, we just skip until[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m639[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m the [0m[35m/[0m[95mCharStrings[0m[39m dict is found[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m640[0m[39m:        while [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.LITERAL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m641[0m[39m:                && [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m642[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m643[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m644[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m645[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/pfb/PfbParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:161[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m168[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m161[0m[39m:            long newTotal = total + size;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m162[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnewTotal > MAX_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m163[0m[39m:                throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"record size would be too large: "[0m[39m + [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnewTotal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m164[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m165[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m166[0m[39m:            byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m ar = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msize[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m167[0m[39m:            int got = [0m[1;35min.read[0m[1;39m([0m[39mar[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m168[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mgot != size[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The hang originates in Type1 parsing when malformed or adversarial PFB/ASCII [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfont data lacks expected sentinel tokens [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., “CharStrings” in ASCII, [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“cleartomark” or equivalent in binary[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Loops in Type1Parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mboth `parseASCII` and `parseBinary`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m do “while [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m!sentinel[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[1;35mnextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m” without detecting EOF or enforcing a maximum number [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof tokens. When the sentinel never appears, `[0m[1;35mnextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` eventually returns null [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrepeatedly, but the loop never breaks, leading to an infinite loop.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The PostScript-tokenization via `Type1Lexer` with its various token kinds [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mSTART_ARRAY, LITERAL, NAME, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing fallback behavior when fonts are damaged [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`DamagedFontException`[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mso PDFBox skips or gracefully handles nonconformant fonts.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - PfbParser’s existing size check [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`MAX_LENGTH`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to guard against excessive [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory usage.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Strategy Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Augment sentinel-search loops in Type1Parser to detect EOF and abort:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. In `[0m[1;35mparseASCII[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, locate the loop around lines [0m[1;36m640[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m645[0m[39m:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         while [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.LITERAL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 && [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Change it to:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         int tokensScanned = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Allow up to [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m× segment length tokens, or use a fixed high watermark[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         int maxTokens = bytes.length * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m1000[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         Token t;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         while [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.LITERAL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  && [0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             t = [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mt == null[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 throw new [0m[1;35mDamagedFontException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Premature EOF while seeking [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m/CharStrings"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m++tokensScanned > maxTokens[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 throw new [0m[1;35mDamagedFontException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Exceeded token limit without [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mfinding /CharStrings"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. In `[0m[1;35mparseBinary[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, identify loops that skip to “cleartomark” [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor other[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbinary-PFB markers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Wrap them similarly: after each `[0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, check for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`null` and count tokens, throwing `DamagedFontException` on EOF or exceeding a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthreshold.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Add a global token‐count limit in Type1Parser.parse[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. At the start of `public Type1Font [0m[1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, insert:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         this.tokenCount = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         this.maxTotalTokens = [0m[1;39m([0m[39msegment1.length + segment2.length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m10000[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. In every invocation of `[0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` inside parse methods, increment[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tokenCount` and if it exceeds `maxTotalTokens`, throw `[0m[1;35mDamagedFontException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Too [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mmany tokens in Type1 parse"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. This ensures any unforeseen loops or missed sentinels still terminate.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Prevent zero‐progress in Type1Lexer.readToken[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Audit fallback code paths in `[0m[1;35mreadToken[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., after failed [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnumeric/name parse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Ensure that every branch either consumes at least one byte or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicitly throws an exception.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. For the “unknown character” default case [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutside defined delimiters[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconvert the character into a single‐character NAME token instead of resetting the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer pointer, guaranteeing forward progress:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Instead of resetting [0m[1;35mbuffer.position[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for unrecognized [0m[32m'<'[0m[39m [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequences,[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m return the single character token and do not revert buffer position.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return new [0m[1;35mToken[0m[1;39m([0m[39mc, Token.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. This change avoids potential backtracking loops where the buffer index [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoes not advance.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Exception and Fallback Flow[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use `DamagedFontException` to indicate parsing failure. This mirrors existing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior for corrupted fonts and lets PDFBox gracefully skip faulty fonts or fall [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mback to alternative rendering.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure that downstream callers of `Type1Parser.parse` catch [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`DamagedFontException` [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready thrown from `Type1Lexer` in some cases[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so PDF [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction does not hang but simply omits text from the damaged font.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Testing and Regression[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add unit tests for:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • A PFB/ASCII segment missing “CharStrings” to assert that [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`DamagedFontException` is thrown within a bounded time.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • A binary segment missing “cleartomark” to trigger the new exception.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • A correctly formed PFB font to verify no regression in normal parsing.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing PDFBox font‐format regression suites to confirm no unintended [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mside‐effects.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introducing EOF checks and token‐count limits ensures that malicious or [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed fonts cannot trigger unbounded loops, resolving the libFuzzer timeout.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Throwing `DamagedFontException` aligns with existing error‐handling patterns. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserves all valid parsing paths and only aborts when progress cannot be [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmade, protecting legitimate fonts.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Avoids changes to harness, fuzzing logic, or external dependencies—only [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtouches core parsing logic.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar guards already exist in PfbParser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mMAX_LENGTH for bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; this extends[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthose protections to token parsing.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
